
\Data\ID{1003124001}
\Updated{2020-07-15 03:07:21}
\Level{A}
\SubArea{Analytic geometry in a space}
\LANGen{
\Question{
We are given a straight line \( q=\left\{[3t;2-2t;1+t]\text{, }t\in\mathbb{R}\right\} \) and four points \( A=[-6;6;-1] \), \( B=[-3;0;0] \), \( C=[0;2;1] \) and \( D=[3;0;2] \). Out of the  given points select all that lie on the straight line \( q \). (Choose the corresponding option.)}
{\( A \), \( C \), \( D \)}{\( B \), \( C \), \( D \)}{\( B \), \( C \)}{\( A \), \( B \), \( C \)}{}{}}
\LANGpl{
\Question{
Dana jest prosta  \( q=\left\{[3t;2-2t;1+t]\text{, }t\in\mathbb{R}\right\} \) oraz cztery punkty \( A=[-6;6;-1] \), \( B=[-3;0;0] \), \( C=[0;2;1] \) i \( D=[3;0;2] \). Z podanych punkt√≥w wybierz wszystkie punkty leŇľńÖce na prostej  \( q \). (Wybierz wŇāaŇõciwńÖ opcje)}
{\( A \), \( C \), \( D \)}{\( B \), \( C \), \( D \)}{\( B \), \( C \)}{\( A \), \( B \), \( C \)}{}{}}
\LANGcs{
\Question{
Je d√°na pŇô√≠mka \( q=\left\{[3t;2-2t;1+t]\text{, }t\in\mathbb{R}\right\} \) a body \( A=[-6;6;-1] \), \( B=[-3;0;0] \), \( C=[0;2;1] \) a \( D=[3;0;2] \). Vyberte z tńõchto ńćtyŇô bodŇĮ vŇ°echny, kter√© leŇĺ√≠ na pŇô√≠mce \( q \), a tuto moŇĺnost oznańćte.}
{\( A \), \( C \), \( D \)}{\( B \), \( C \), \( D \)}{\( B \), \( C \)}{\( A \), \( B \), \( C \)}{}{}}
\LANGsk{
\Question{
Je dan√° priamka \( q=\left\{[3t;2-2t;1+t]\text{, }t\in\mathbb{R}\right\} \) a body \( A=[-6;6;-1] \), \( B=[-3;0;0] \), \( C=[0;2;1] \) a \( D=[3;0;2] \). Vyberte z t√Ĺchto Ň°tyroch bodov vŇ°etky, ktor√© leŇĺia na priamke \( q \), a t√ļto moŇĺnosŇ• oznańćte.}
{\( A \), \( C \), \( D \)}{\( B \), \( C \), \( D \)}{\( B \), \( C \)}{\( A \), \( B \), \( C \)}{}{}}
\LANGes{
\Question{
Dada la recta \( q=\left\{[3t;2-2t;1+t]\text{, }t\in\mathbb{R}\right\} \) y los puntos  \( A=[-6;6;-1] \), \( B=[-3;0;0] \), \( C=[0;2;1] \) y \( D=[3;0;2] \). Determina cu√°les de estos cuatro puntos pertenecen a la recta q. Elige la opci√≥n correcta.}
{\( A \), \( C \), \( D \)}{\( B \), \( C \), \( D \)}{\( B \), \( C \)}{\( A \), \( B \), \( C \)}{}{}}
\End

\SubArea{Analytic geometry in a space}
\LANGen{
\Question{
From the given options choose the parametric equations which describe a straight line \( p \) passing through the points \( A=[-2;0;1] \) and \( B=[2;0;-3] \).}
{\( \begin{aligned}
p\colon x&=2-t, \\
y&=0, \\
z&=-3+t;\ t\in\mathbb{R}
\end{aligned} \)}{\( \begin{aligned}
p\colon x&=2+4t, \\
y&=0, \\
z&=-3+4t;\ t\in\mathbb{R}
\end{aligned} \)}{\( \begin{aligned}
p\colon x&=2, \\
y&=0, \\
z&=-3+t;\ t\in\mathbb{R}
\end{aligned} \)}{\( \begin{aligned}
p\colon x&=2-2t, \\
y&=0, \\
z&=-3+t;\ t\in\mathbb{R}
\end{aligned} \)}{}{}}
\LANGpl{
\Question{
Wybierz r√≥wnanie parametryczne prostej \( p \) przechodzńÖcej przez punkty  \( A=[-2;0;1] \) i \( B=[2;0;-3] \).}
{\( \begin{aligned}

\end{aligned} \)}{\( \begin{aligned}

\end{aligned} \)}{\( \begin{aligned}

\end{aligned} \)}{\( \begin{aligned}
p\colon x&=2-2t, \\
y&=0, \\
z&=-3+t;\ t\in\mathbb{R}
\end{aligned} \)}{}{}}

\end{aligned} \)}{\( \begin{aligned}

\end{aligned} \)}{\( \begin{aligned}

\end{aligned} \)}{\( \begin{aligned}
p\colon x&=2-2t, \\

\end{aligned} \)}{}{}}
\LANGsk{

Z pon√ļknut√Ĺch moŇĺnost√≠ vyberte parametrick√© rovnice, ktor√© urńćuj√ļ priamku \( p \) prech√°dzaj√ļcu bodmi \( A=[-2;0;1] \) a \( B=[2;0;-3] \).}

\end{aligned} \)}{\( \begin{aligned}

\Data\ID{1003124003}
\Updated{2020-07-15 03:07:21}
\Level{A}
\SubArea{Analytic geometry in a space}
\LANGen{
\Question{
Find the missing coordinates of the point \( B=[x_B; y_B;-3] \) lying on a straight line \( p \) defined by the parametric equations \[\begin{aligned} p\colon x&=-1+\frac14m,\\ y&=2+m,\\ z&=5-m;\ m\in\mathbb{R}.\end{aligned} \]}
{\( B=[1;10;-3] \)}{\( B=[-3;-6;-3] \)}{\( B=[1;3;-3] \)}{\( B=[-3;6;-3] \)}{}{}}
\LANGpl{
\Question{
WskaŇľ brakujńÖce wsp√≥Ňārzńôdne punktu \( B=[x_B; y_B;-3] \) lezńÖcego na prostej \( p \) okreŇõlonej r√≥wnaniem parametrycznym \[\begin{aligned}p\colon x&=-1+\frac14m,\\ y&=2+m,\\ z&=5-m;\ m\in\mathbb{R}.\end{aligned} \]}
{\( B=[1;10;-3] \)}{\( B=[-3;-6;-3] \)}{\( B=[1;3;-3] \)}{\( B=[-3;6;-3] \)}{}{}}
\LANGcs{
\Question{
Urńćete chybńõj√≠c√≠ souŇôadnice bodu \( B=[x_B; y_B;-3] \) leŇĺ√≠c√≠ho na pŇô√≠mce \( p \) s parametrick√Ĺm vyj√°dŇôen√≠m: \[\begin{aligned} x&=-1+\frac14m,\\ y&=2+m,\\ z&=5-m;\ m\in\mathbb{R}\end{aligned} \]}
{\( B=[1;10;-3] \)}{\( B=[-3;-6;-3] \)}{\( B=[1;3;-3] \)}{\( B=[-3;6;-3] \)}{}{}}
\LANGsk{
\Question{
Urńćte ch√Ĺbaj√ļce s√ļradnice bodov \( B=[x_B; y_B;-3] \) leŇĺiaceho na priamke \( p \) s parametrick√Ĺm vyjadren√≠m: 
\[\begin{aligned} x&=-1+\frac14m,\\ y&=2+m,\\ z&=5-m;\ m\in\mathbb{R}\end{aligned} \]}
{\( B=[1;10;-3] \)}{\( B=[-3;-6;-3] \)}{\( B=[1;3;-3] \)}{\( B=[-3;6;-3] \)}{}{}}
\LANGes{
\Question{
Halla las coordenadas del punto \( B=[x_B; y_B;-3] \) que pertenece a la recta \( p \) definida por las siguientes ecuaciones param√©tricas: \[\begin{aligned} p\colon x&=-1+\frac14m,\\ y&=2+m,\\ z&=5-m;\ m\in\mathbb{R}.\end{aligned} \]}
{\( B=[1;10;-3] \)}{\( B=[-3;-6;-3] \)}{\( B=[1;3;-3] \)}{\( B=[-3;6;-3] \)}{}{}}
\End

\Data\ID{1003124004}
\Updated{2020-07-15 03:07:21}
\Level{A}
\SubArea{Analytic geometry in a space}
\LANGen{
\Question{
Find the value of a parameter \( a\in\mathbb{R} \) so that the point \( B=[1;4;5] \) lies on the straight line \( p \) defined by the parametric equations \[\begin{aligned}p\colon x&=-1+m,\\ y&=2+am,\\ z&=3+m;\ m\in\mathbb{R}. \end{aligned}\]}
{\( a=1 \)}{\( a=-1 \)}{\( a=2 \)}{no such value of \( a \) exists}{}{}}
\LANGpl{
\Question{
WskaŇľ wartoŇõńá parametru  \( a\in\mathbb{R} \) tak, aby punkt  \( B=[1;4;5] \) leŇľaŇā na prostej  \( p \) okreŇõlonej r√≥wnaniem parametryczny \[\begin{aligned} p\colon x&=-1+m,\\ y&=2+am,\\ z&=3+m;\ m\in\mathbb{R}. \end{aligned}\]}
{\( a=1 \)}{\( a=-1 \)}{\( a=2 \)}{wartoŇõńá parametru \( a \) nie istnieje}{}{}}
\LANGcs{
\Question{
Urńćete hodnotu parametru \( a\in\mathbb{R} \) tak, aby bod \( B=[1;4;5] \) leŇĺel na pŇô√≠mce \( p \) s parametrick√Ĺm vyj√°dŇôen√≠m: \[\begin{aligned} x&=-1+m,\\ y&=2+am,\\ z&=3+m;\ m\in\mathbb{R} \end{aligned}\]}
{\( a=1 \)}{\( a=-1 \)}{\( a=2 \)}{takov√° hodnota \( a \) neexistuje}{}{}}
\LANGsk{
\Question{
Urńćte hodnotu parametra \( a\in\mathbb{R} \) tak, aby bod \( B=[1;4;5] \) leŇĺal na priamke \( p \) s parametrick√Ĺm vyjadren√≠m: \[\begin{aligned} x&=-1+m,\\ y&=2+am,\\ z&=3+m;\ m\in\mathbb{R} \end{aligned}\]}
{\( a=1 \)}{\( a=-1 \)}{\( a=2 \)}{tak√° hodnota \( a \) neexistuje}{}{}}
\LANGes{
\Question{
Halla el valor del par√°metro  \( a\in\mathbb{R} \) de modo que el punto \( B=[1;4;5] \) pertenezca a la recta  \( p \), la cual tiene las siguientes ecuaciones param√©tricas:  \[\begin{aligned}p\colon x&=-1+m,\\ y&=2+am,\\ z&=3+m;\ m\in\mathbb{R}. \end{aligned}\]}
{\( a=1 \)}{\( a=-1 \)}{\( a=2 \)}{este valor \( a \) no existe}{}{}}
\End

\Data\ID{1003164401}
\Updated{2020-07-15 03:07:21}
\Level{A}
\SubArea{Analytic geometry in a space}
\LANGen{
\Question{
Let a straight line \( p \) be defined by parametric equations:
\begin{align*}
x&=-1+2t, \\
y&=2+t, \\
z&=5-t;\ t\in\mathbb{R}.
\end{align*} 
Find the coordinates of the intersection point \( M \) of the line \( p \) with the \( xy \)-coordinate plane.}
{\( M=[9;7;0] \)}{\( M=[0;0;5] \)}{\( M=[-1;2;0] \)}{\( M=[0;0;-1] \)}{}{}}
\LANGpl{
\Question{
Dana jest prosta  \( p \) okreŇõlona r√≥wnaniem parametrycznym:
\begin{align*}
x&=-1+2t, \\
y&=2+t, \\
z&=5-t;\ t\in\mathbb{R}.
\end{align*} 
WskaŇľ wsp√≥Ňārzńôdne punktu \( M \), kt√≥ry jest punktem przecińôcia prostej  \( p \) z pŇāaszczyznńÖ w ukŇāadzie wsp√≥Ňārzńôdnych \( xy \).}
{\( M=[9;7;0] \)}{\( M=[0;0;5] \)}{\( M=[-1;2;0] \)}{\( M=[0;0;-1] \)}{}{}}
\LANGcs{
\Question{
PŇô√≠mka \( p \) je zad√°na sv√Ĺm parametrick√Ĺm vyj√°dŇôen√≠m:
\begin{align*}
x&=-1+2t, \\
y&=2+t, \\
z&=5-t;\ t\in\mathbb{R}.
\end{align*} 
Urńćete souŇôadnice bodu \( M \), ve kter√©m pŇô√≠mka \( p \) prot√≠n√° souŇôadnou rovinu \( (xy) \).}
{\( M=[9;7;0] \)}{\( M=[0;0;5] \)}{\( M=[-1;2;0] \)}{\( M=[0;0;-1] \)}{}{}}
\LANGsk{
\Question{
Priamka \( p \) je zadan√° svoj√≠m parametrick√Ĺm vyjadren√≠m:
\begin{align*}
x&=-1+2t, \\
y&=2+t, \\
z&=5-t;\ t\in\mathbb{R}.
\end{align*} 
Urńćte s√ļradnice bodu \( M \), v ktorom priamka \( p \) pret√≠na s√ļradnicov√ļ rovinu \( (xy) \).}
{\( M=[9;7;0] \)}{\( M=[0;0;5] \)}{\( M=[-1;2;0] \)}{\( M=[0;0;-1] \)}{}{}}
\LANGes{
\Question{
Dada la recta \( p \) cuyas ecuaciones param√©tricas son:
\begin{align*}
x&=-1+2t, \\
y&=2+t, \\
z&=5-t;\ t\in\mathbb{R}.
\end{align*} 
Encuentra las coordenadas del punto \( M \), intersecci√≥n de la recta \( p \) el plano de coordenadas \( xy \).}
{\( M=[9;7;0] \)}{\( M=[0;0;5] \)}{\( M=[-1;2;0] \)}{\( M=[0;0;-1] \)}{}{}}
\End

\Data\ID{1003164402}
\Updated{2020-07-15 03:07:21}
\Level{A}
\SubArea{Analytic geometry in a space}
\LANGen{
\Question{
Let a straight line \( p \) be defined by parametric equations:
\begin{align*}
x&=-1+2t, \\
y&=2+t, \\
z&=5-t;\ t\in\mathbb{R}.
\end{align*}

{\( M=[-5;0;7] \)}{\( M=[0;2;0] \)}{\( M=[-1;0;5] \)}{\( M=[2;0;-1] \)}{}{}}
\LANGpl{
\Question{
Dana jest prosta  \( p \) okreŇõlona r√≥wnaniem parametrycznym:
\begin{align*}
x&=-1+2t, \\

z&=5-t,\ t\in\mathbb{R}.
\end{align*} 
WskaŇľ wsp√≥Ňārzńôdne punktu  \( M \), kt√≥ry jest punktem przecińôcia prostej \( p \) z pŇāaszczyznńÖ w ukŇāadzie wsp√≥Ňārzńôdnych \( xz \).}
{\( M=[-5;0;7] \)}{\( M=[0;2;0] \)}{\( M=[-1;0;5] \)}{\( M=[2;0;-1] \)}{}{}}
\LANGcs{
\Question{
PŇô√≠mka \( p \) je zad√°na sv√Ĺm parametrick√Ĺm vyj√°dŇôen√≠m:
\begin{align*}
x&=-1+2t, \\
y&=2+t, \\
z&=5-t,\ t\in\mathbb{R}.
\end{align*}

{\( M=[-5;0;7] \)}{\( M=[0;2;0] \)}{\( M=[-1;0;5] \)}{\( M=[2;0;-1] \)}{}{}}
\LANGsk{
\Question{
Priamka \( p \) je zadan√° svoj√≠m parametrick√Ĺm vyjadren√≠m:
\begin{align*}
x&=-1+2t, \\
y&=2+t, \\
z&=5-t,\ t\in\mathbb{R}.
\end{align*} 
Urńćte s√ļradnice bodu \( M \), v ktorom priamka \( p \) pret√≠na s√ļradnicov√ļ rovinu \( (xz) \).}
{\( M=[-5;0;7] \)}{\( M=[0;2;0] \)}{\( M=[-1;0;5] \)}{\( M=[2;0;-1] \)}{}{}}
\LANGes{
\Question{
Dada la recta \( p \) cuyas ecuaciones param√©tricas son:
\begin{align*}
x&=-1+2t, \\
y&=2+t, \\
z&=5-t;\ t\in\mathbb{R}.
\end{align*} 
Encuentra las coordenadas del punto \( M \), intersecci√≥n de la recta \( p \) y el plano de coordenadas \( xz \).}
{\( M=[-5;0;7] \)}{\( M=[0;2;0] \)}{\( M=[-1;0;5] \)}{\( M=[2;0;-1] \)}{}{}}
\End

\LANGen{
\Question{

\end{align*}

\Question{

\begin{align*}

\end{align*}}

\end{align*}}

\end{align*}}

\Data\ID{1003188906}
\Updated{2020-07-15 03:07:21}
\Level{A}
\SubArea{Analytic geometry in a space}
\LANGen{
\Question{
Let there be planes \( \alpha \), \( \beta \), \( \gamma \) and \( \delta \) defined by their general equations:  
\[ \begin{aligned}
&\alpha\colon \frac23x-4y+6z-\frac83=0; \\
&\beta\colon x-2y+3z-4=0; \\
&\gamma\colon 2x-12y+18z-4 =0; \\
&\delta\colon x-6y+9z-4 =0.
\end{aligned} \]
Out of the following statements, select the one that is not true.}
{\( \alpha \parallel\delta\text{, }\alpha\neq\delta \)}{Planes \( \beta \) and \( \delta \) are intersecting.}{\( \gamma\parallel\delta\text{, }\gamma\neq\delta \)}{Planes \( \alpha \) and \( \beta \) are intersecting.}{\( \alpha = \delta \)}{}}
\LANGpl{
\Question{
PŇāaszczyzny  \( \alpha \), \( \beta \), \( \gamma \) i \( \delta \) sńÖ okreŇõlone r√≥wnaniami og√≥lnymi:  
\[ \begin{aligned}
&\alpha\colon \frac23x-4y+6z-\frac83=0; \\
&\beta\colon x-2y+3z-4=0; \\
&\gamma\colon 2x-12y+18z-4 =0; \\
&\delta\colon x-6y+9z-4 =0.
\end{aligned} \]
Z poniŇľszych stwierdzeŇĄ, wybierz t nieprawdziwe.}
{\( \alpha \parallel\delta\text{, }\alpha\neq\delta \)}{PŇāaszczyzny  \( \beta \) i \( \delta \) przecinajńÖ sińô.}{\( \gamma\parallel\delta\text{, }\gamma\neq\delta \)}{PŇāaszczyzny \( \alpha \) i \( \beta \) przecinajńÖ sińô.}{\( \alpha = \delta \)}{}}
\LANGcs{
\Question{
Roviny \( \alpha \), \( \beta \), \( \gamma \) a \( \delta \) jsou d√°ny sv√Ĺmi obecn√Ĺmi rovnicemi:  
\[ \begin{aligned}
&\alpha\colon \frac23x-4y+6z-\frac83=0; \\
&\beta\colon x-2y+3z-4=0; \\
&\gamma\colon 2x-12y+18z-4 =0; \\
&\delta\colon x-6y+9z-4 =0.
\end{aligned} \]
Urńćete, kter√© z n√°sleduj√≠c√≠ch tvrzen√≠ nen√≠ pravdiv√©.}
{\( \alpha \parallel\delta\text{, }\alpha\neq\delta \)}{Roviny \( \beta \) a \( \delta \) jsou rŇĮznobńõŇĺn√©.}{\( \gamma\parallel\delta\text{, }\gamma\neq\delta \)}{Roviny \( \alpha \) a \( \beta \) jsou rŇĮznobńõŇĺn√©.}{\( \alpha = \delta \)}{}}
\LANGsk{
\Question{
Roviny \( \alpha \), \( \beta \), \( \gamma \) a \( \delta \) s√ļ dan√© svojimi vŇ°eobecn√Ĺmi rovnicami:  
\[ \begin{aligned}
&\alpha\colon \frac23x-4y+6z-\frac83=0; \\
&\beta\colon x-2y+3z-4=0; \\
&\gamma\colon 2x-12y+18z-4 =0; \\
&\delta\colon x-6y+9z-4 =0.
\end{aligned} \]
Urńćte, ktor√© z nasleduj√ļcich tvrden√≠ nie je pravdiv√©.}
{\( \alpha \parallel\delta\text{, }\alpha\neq\delta \)}{Roviny \( \beta \) a \( \delta \) s√ļ r√īznobeŇĺn√©.}{\( \gamma\parallel\delta\text{, }\gamma\neq\delta \)}{Roviny \( \alpha \) a \( \beta \) s√ļ r√īznobeŇĺn√©.}{\( \alpha = \delta \)}{}}
\LANGes{
\Question{
Dados los planos \( \alpha \), \( \beta \), \( \gamma \) y \( \delta \) cuyas ecuaciones generales son:   
\[ \begin{aligned}
&\alpha\colon \frac23x-4y+6z-\frac83=0; \\
&\beta\colon x-2y+3z-4=0; \\
&\gamma\colon 2x-12y+18z-4 =0; \\
&\delta\colon x-6y+9z-4 =0.
\end{aligned} \]
Determina cu√°l de las siguientes afirmaciones no es verdadera:}
{\( \alpha \parallel\delta\text{, }\alpha\neq\delta \)}{Los planos \( \beta \) y \( \delta \) no son paralelos.}{\( \gamma\parallel\delta\text{, }\gamma\neq\delta \)}{Los planos \( \alpha \) y \( \beta \) no son paralelos.}{\( \alpha = \delta \)}{}}
\End

\Question{

\end{aligned}$}{$\begin{aligned}

\end{aligned}$}{$\begin{aligned}
p\colon x&=4+2t, \\
y&=7+3t, \\
z&=6;\ t\in\mathbb{R}
\end{aligned}$}{$\begin{aligned}
p\colon x&=2-2t, \\
y&=4-3t, \\
z&=-6t;\ t\in\mathbb{R}
\end{aligned}$}{}{}}
\LANGpl{
\Question{
Dane sńÖ punkty \( A=[2;4;0] \) and \( B=[4;7;6] \). WskaŇľ r√≥wnanie parametryczne prostej \( q \), kt√≥ra jest rzutem prostokńÖtnym prostej \( AB \) na pŇāaszczyŇļnie w ukŇāadzie wsp√≥Ňārzńôdnych \( xy \).}
{$\begin{aligned}
p\colon x&=4+2t, \\
y&=7+3t, \\
z&=0;\ t\in\mathbb{R}
\end{aligned}$}{$\begin{aligned}
p\colon x&=2+4t, \\
y&=4+7t, \\
z&=6t;\ t\in\mathbb{R}
\end{aligned}$}{$\begin{aligned}
p\colon x&=4+2t, \\
y&=7+3t, \\
z&=6;\ t\in\mathbb{R}
\end{aligned}$}{$\begin{aligned}

\Data\ID{9000101004}
\Updated{2020-09-01 09:09:23}
\Level{A}
\SubArea{Analytic geometry in a space}
\LANGen{
\Question{
Find all the values of the real parameter  \(m\) 
so that  the lines \(p\) 
and \(q\) 
are skew lines. 
\[ 
\begin{aligned}p\colon x& = 1 + t, &
\\y & = 2 - t,
\\z & = 1 - t;\ t\in \mathbb{R}
\\ \end{aligned}\qquad \qquad \begin{aligned}q\colon x& = s, &
\\y & = 1 + s,
\\z & = 3 + ms;\ s\in \mathbb{R}
\\ \end{aligned}
\]}
{\(m\in\mathbb{R}\setminus\{-2\}\)}{No solution exists.}{The lines are skew for every real \(m\).}{\(m = -2\)}{}{}}
\LANGpl{
\Question{
Wyznacz rzeczywistńÖ wartoŇõńá parametru \(m\) 
tak, aby proste \(p\) 
i \(q\) 
byŇāy prostymi skoŇõnymi. 
\[ 
\begin{aligned}p\colon x& = 1 + t, &
\\y & = 2 - t,
\\z & = 1 - t;\ t\in \mathbb{R}
\\ \end{aligned}\qquad \qquad \begin{aligned}q\colon x& = s, &
\\y & = 1 + s,
\\z & = 3 + ms;\ s\in \mathbb{R}
\\ \end{aligned}
\]}
{\(m\in\mathbb{R}\setminus\{-2\}\)}{Brak rozwińÖzania.}{Proste sńÖ skoŇõne dla kaŇľdej  rzeczywistej wartoŇõci  \(m\).}{\(m = -2\)}{}{}}

\[

\[ 
\begin{aligned}[t] p\colon x& = -6 - t,&

\\z & = 10 - 4s;\ s\in \mathbb{R}

\]}

{4}y + \frac{2} 
{3}z -\frac{2} 
{5} = 0,\qquad \sigma \colon \frac{2}
{3}x - 4y + \frac{3} 
{2}z -\frac{5} 
{2} = 0 & &
\end{aligned}\]}
{przecinajńÖce sińô}{pokrywajńÖce sińô}{r√≥wnolegŇāe, nie pokrywajńÖce sińô}{}{}{}}

\Question{

 \begin{align*}

z&=4-t;\ t\in\mathbb{R},
\end{align*}

{\( \alpha\colon x+2y-z+3=0;\ B=[6;-2;5] \)}{\( \alpha\colon x+2y-z-3;\ B=[6;-2;5] \)}{\( \alpha\colon x+2y-z-3=0;\ B=[8;2;3] \)}{\( \alpha\colon x+2y-z+3=0;\ B=[8;2;3] \)}{}{}}

\Question{

y&=2t, \\ 
z&=4-t;\ t\in\mathbb{R},
\end{align*}
a proch√°z√≠ bodem \( A=[1;0;4] \). D√°le vypońćtńõte souŇôadnice bodu \( B \), ve kter√©m pŇô√≠mka \( p \) prot√≠n√° rovinu \( \alpha \) (viz obr√°zek).}

\\ \end{aligned}\)}{}{}}

obecnou rovnic√≠: \(2x + y - z - 5 = 0\).

{\(\gamma \colon 3x - 2 = 0\)}{\(\beta \colon 2z - 2 = 0\)}{\(\alpha \colon x + y - 2 = 0\)}{}{}{}}

\Data\ID{1003233607}

\Level{C}
\SubArea{Analytic geometry in a space}
\LANGen{
\Question{
Determine the relative position of three planes:
\begin{align*}
\alpha\colon\ &2x+y+9z-18=0, \\
\beta\colon\ &x+3y+2z+16=0, \\
\gamma\colon\ &x+2y+3z+6=0.
\end{align*}}
{Planes $\alpha$, $\beta$ and $\gamma$ intersect in a straight line.}{Each of the two planes are intersecting and the lines of intersection are three different lines parallel  to each other.}{All three planes intersect at just one point.}{}{}{}}
\LANGpl{
\Question{
OkreŇõl wzajemne poŇāoŇľenie trzech pŇāaszczyzn:
\begin{align*}
\alpha\colon\ &2x+y+9z-18=0, \\
\beta\colon\ &x+3y+2z+16=0, \\
\gamma\colon\ &x+2y+3z+6=0.
\end{align*}}
{PŇāaszczyzny $\alpha$, $\beta$ i $\gamma$ przecinajńÖ sińô na prostej.}{KaŇľda z dw√≥ch pŇāaszczyzn przecina sińô, a proste przecińôcia to trzy r√≥Ňľne proste r√≥wnolegŇāe do siebie.}{Trzy pŇāaszczyzny przecinajńÖ sińô w jednym punkcie.}{}{}{}}
\LANGcs{
\Question{
Urńćete vz√°jemnou polohu tŇô√≠ rovin:
\begin{align*}
\alpha\colon\ &2x+y+9z-18=0, \\
\beta\colon\ &x+3y+2z+16=0, \\
\gamma\colon\ &x+2y+3z+6=0.
\end{align*}}

\Question{
A cube \( ABCDEFGH \) with an edge length of \( 2 \) is placed in a coordinate system (see the picture). Let the point \( M \) be the centre of the edge \( EF \). Find the general form equation of the plane \( \rho \) passing through the points \( B \), \( D \), and \( G \) and calculate the distance of \( M \) from the plane \( \rho \).}
{\( \rho\colon x-y+z=0;\ |M\rho|=\sqrt3 \)}{\( \rho\colon x-y+z+2=0;\ |M\rho|=\sqrt3 \)}{\( \rho\colon x-y+z+2=0;\ |M\rho|=2\sqrt3 \)}{\( \rho\colon x-y+z=0;\ |M\rho|=2\sqrt3 \)}{}{}}
\LANGpl{
\Question{
SzeŇõcian \( ABCDEFGH \) o krawńôdzi r√≥wnej \( 2 \) znajduje sińô w ukŇāadzie wsp√≥Ňārzńôdnych  (sp√≥jrz na rysunek). Punkt \( M \) to Ňõrodek krawńôdzi \( EF \). {\( \rho\colon x-y+z=0;\ |M\rho|=\sqrt3 \)}{\( \rho\colon x-y+z+2=0;\ |M\rho|=\sqrt3 \)}{\( \rho\colon x-y+z+2=0;\ |M\rho|=2\sqrt3 \)}{\( \rho\colon x-y+z=0;\ |M\rho|=2\sqrt3 \)}{}{}}
\LANGcs{
\Question{
Krychle \( ABCDEFGH \) s d√©lkou hrany \( 2 \) je um√≠stńõna v souŇôadn√©m syst√©mu (viz obr√°zek). Bod \( M \) je stŇôed hrany \( EF \). Urńćete obecnou rovnici roviny \( \rho \) proch√°zej√≠c√≠ body \( B \), \( D \) a \( G \) a vypońćtńõte vzd√°lenost bodu \( M \) od roviny \( \rho \).}
{\( \rho\colon x-y+z=0;\ |M\rho|=\sqrt3 \)}{\( \rho\colon x-y+z+2=0;\ |M\rho|=\sqrt3 \)}{\( \rho\colon x-y+z+2=0;\ |M\rho|=2\sqrt3 \)}{\( \rho\colon x-y+z=0;\ |M\rho|=2\sqrt3 \)}{}{}}
\LANGsk{
\Question{
Kocka \( ABCDEFGH \) s dńļŇĺkou hrany \( 2 \) je umiestnen√° v s√ļradnicovom syst√©mu (vińŹ obr√°zok). Bod \( M \) je stred hrany \( EF \). Urńćte vŇ°eobecn√ļ rovnicu roviny \( \rho \) prech√°dzaj√ļcu bodmi \( B \), \( D \) a \( G \) a vypońć√≠tajte vzdialenosŇ• bodu \( M \) od roviny \( \rho \).}

\LANGes{

\Level{C}
\SubArea{Analytic geometry in a space}
\IMG{1103212205.pdf}
\LANGen{
\Question{
A cube \( ABCDEFGH \) with an edge length of \( 2 \) is placed in a coordinate system (see the picture). Find the distance between parallel planes \( \alpha \) and \( \beta \), where \( \alpha \) is passing through \( B \), \( D \) and \( G \) and \( \beta \) is passing through \( A \), \( F \) and \( H \).}
{\( |\alpha\beta|=\frac{2\sqrt3}3 \)}{\( |\alpha\beta|=\frac{4\sqrt3}3 \)}{\( |\alpha\beta|=\frac{3\sqrt3}2 \)}{\( |\alpha\beta|=\frac{3\sqrt3}4 \)}{}{}}
\LANGpl{
\Question{
SzeŇõcian \( ABCDEFGH \) o krawńôdzi r√≥wnej  \( 2 \) znajduje sińô w ukŇāadzie wsp√≥Ňārzńôdnych  (sp√≥jrz na rysunek). Oblicz odlegŇāoŇõńá pomińôdzy r√≥wnolegŇāymi pŇāaszczyznami \( \alpha \) i \( \beta \), gdzie \( \alpha \) przechodzi przez\( B \), \( D \) i \( G \) a \( \beta \) przechodzi przez \( A \), \( F \) i \( H \).}
{\( |\alpha\beta|=\frac{2\sqrt3}3 \)}{\( |\alpha\beta|=\frac{4\sqrt3}3 \)}{\( |\alpha\beta|=\frac{3\sqrt3}2 \)}{\( |\alpha\beta|=\frac{3\sqrt3}4 \)}{}{}}

\LANGen{
\Question{
A cube \( ABCDEFGH \) with an edge length of \( 2 \) units is placed in a coordinate system (see the picture). Find an angle \( \varphi \) between the plane \( \alpha \) passing through the points \( E \), \( D \) and \( C \) and the straight line \( AF \).

Hint: An angle between a line and a plane is an angle between the line and its orthogonal projection into this plane.}
{\( \varphi = 30^{\circ} \)}{\( \varphi = 15^{\circ} \)}{\( \varphi = 45^{\circ} \)}{\( \varphi = 60^{\circ} \)}{}{}}
\LANGpl{
\Question{
SzeŇõcian \( ABCDEFGH \) o dŇāugoŇõci krawńôdzi r√≥wnej \( 2 \) jednostki zostaŇā umieszczony w ukŇāadzie wsp√≥Ňārzńôdnych (sp√≥jrz na rysunek). Wyznacz kńÖt \( \varphi \) pomińôdzy pŇāaszczyznńÖ \( \alpha \) przechodzńÖcńÖ przez punkty \( E \), \( D \) i \( C \) a prostńÖ  \( AF \).

Wskaz√≥wka: KńÖt pomińôdzy prostńÖ a pŇāaszczyznńÖ to kńÖt pomińôdzy prostńÖ a jej rzutem prostopadŇāym na pŇāaszczyznńô.}
{\( \varphi = 30^{\circ} \)}{\( \varphi = 15^{\circ} \)}{\( \varphi = 45^{\circ} \)}{\( \varphi = 60^{\circ} \)}{}{}}
\LANGcs{
\Question{
Krychle \( ABCDEFGH \) s d√©lkou hrany \( 2 \) je um√≠stńõna v souŇôadn√©m syst√©mu (viz obr√°zek). Vypońćtńõte odchylku \( \varphi \) pŇô√≠mky \( AF \) od roviny \( \alpha \) proch√°zej√≠c√≠ body \( E \), \( D \) a \( C \).

N√°povńõda: Odchylka pŇô√≠mky od roviny je odchylka pŇô√≠mky od jej√≠ho kolm√©ho prŇĮmńõtu do t√©to roviny.}
{\( \varphi = 30^{\circ} \)}{\( \varphi = 15^{\circ} \)}{\( \varphi = 45^{\circ} \)}{\( \varphi = 60^{\circ} \)}{}{}}
\LANGsk{
\Question{
Kocka \( ABCDEFGH \) s dńļŇĺkou hrany \( 2 \) je umiestnen√° v s√ļradnicovom syst√©me (vińŹ obr√°zok). Vypońć√≠tajte odch√Ĺlku \( \varphi \) priamky \( AF \) od roviny \( \alpha \) prech√°dzaj√ļcej bodmi \( E \), \( D \) a \( C \).

N√°poveda: Odch√Ĺlka priamky od roviny je odch√Ĺlka priamky od jej kolm√©ho priemetu do tejto roviny.}
{\( \varphi = 30^{\circ} \)}{\( \varphi = 15^{\circ} \)}{\( \varphi = 45^{\circ} \)}{\( \varphi = 60^{\circ} \)}{}{}}
\LANGes{
\Question{
Sea \( ABCDEFGH \) el cubo cuya longitud de la arista es \( 2 \) (mira la imagen). Determina el √°ngulo \( \varphi \) formado entre la recta \( AF \) y el plano \( \alpha \) que pasa por los puntos \( E \), \( D \) y \( C \).

Pista: El √°ngulo formado entre una recta y un plano es igual al √°ngulo formado entre la proyecci√≥n perpendicular de la recta en el plano.}
{\( \varphi = 30^{\circ} \)}{\( \varphi = 15^{\circ} \)}{\( \varphi = 45^{\circ} \)}{\( \varphi = 60^{\circ} \)}{}{}}
\End

\LANGen{
\Question{
A rectangle-based right pyramid \( ABCDV \) with a bottom edge length of \( 6 \) units and the perpendicular height of \( 6 \) units is placed in a coordinate system (see the picture). Let \( S \) be the midpoint of the edge \( AD \). Find the standard equation of the plane \( \alpha \) passing through the points \( B \), \( V \) and \( C \), and calculate the distance of the point \( S \) from \( \alpha \).}
{\( \alpha\colon 2y+z-12=0;\ d=|S\alpha|=\frac{12\sqrt5}{5} \)}{\( \alpha\colon 2x+z-12=0;\ d=|S\alpha|=\frac{12\sqrt5}{5} \)}{\( \alpha\colon 2y+z-12=0;\ d=|S\alpha|=\frac{6\sqrt5}{5} \)}{\( \alpha\colon 2x+z-12=0;\ d=|S\alpha|=\frac{6\sqrt5}{5} \)}{}{}}
\LANGpl{
\Question{
Dany jest ostrosŇāup  \( ABCDV \), kt√≥rego podstawńÖ jest prostokńÖt, dŇāugoŇõńá podstawy jest r√≥wna   \( 6 \) jednostek, jego wysokoŇõńá jest r√≥wna \( 6 \) jednostek. OstrosŇāup zostaŇā umieszczony w ukŇāadzie wsp√≥Ňārzńôdnych  (sp√≥jrz na rysunek). Punkt \( S \) to Ňõrodek krawńôdzi \( AD \). Wyznacz r√≥wnanie pŇāaszczyzny  \( \alpha \) przechodzńÖcej przez punkty  \( B \), \( V \) i \( C \) oraz oblicz odlegŇāoŇõńá punktu \( S \) od \( \alpha \).}

\LANGen{
\Question{
In the plane symmetry (reflection) defined by the plane
\(\alpha \),
\[ 
 \alpha \colon 2x + y - z - 5 = 0,
\]
find the image \(A'\) 
of the point \(A = [0;0;1]\).}
{\(A' = [4;2;-1]\)}{\(A' = [6;3;-2]\)}{\(A' = [4;2;1]\)}{\(A' = [0;0;1]\)}{}{}}
\LANGpl{
\Question{
Na pŇāaszczyŇļnie symetrii okreŇõlonej pŇāaszczyznńÖ 
\(\alpha \),
\[ 
 \alpha \colon 2x + y - z - 5 = 0,
\]
wyznacz  wsp√≥Ňārzńôdne punktu \(A'\) 
bńôdńÖcego obrazem \(A = [0;0;1]\).}
{\(A' = [4;2;-1]\)}{\(A' = [6;3;-2]\)}{\(A' = [4;2;1]\)}{\(A' = [0;0;1]\)}{}{}}
\LANGcs{
\Question{
Rovina \(\alpha \) je zadan√°
obecnou rovnic√≠: \(2x + y - z - 5 = 0\). Urńćete
souŇôadnice bodu \(A'\), kter√Ĺ je
obrazem bodu \(A = [0;0;1]\) v rovinov√©
soumńõrnosti podle roviny \(\alpha \).}
{\(A' = [4;2;-1]\)}{\(A' = [6;3;-2]\)}{\(A' = [4;2;1]\)}{\(A' = [0;0;1]\)}{}{}}
\LANGsk{

vŇ°eobecnou rovnicou: \(2x + y - z - 5 = 0\). Urńćte
s√ļradnice bodu \(A'\), ktor√Ĺ je

{\(A' = [4;2;-1]\)}{\(A' = [6;3;-2]\)}{\(A' = [4;2;1]\)}{\(A' = [0;0;1]\)}{}{}}

\SubArea{Analytic geometry in a space}
\IMG{001063_07-figure0.pdf}
\LANGen{
\Question{
Given points \(A = [0;0;1]\),
\(B = [2;0;-1]\) and
\(S = [2;1;0]\),
find the parametric equations of the image of the line
\(AB\) in a point reflection
about the point \(S\).}
{\(\begin{aligned}[t] x& =\phantom{ -}4 + t, &
\\y& =\phantom{ -}2,
\\z& = -1 - t;\ t\in \mathbb{R}
\\ \end{aligned}\)}{\(\begin{aligned}[t] x& = 2 + 2m, &
\\y& = 2 +\phantom{ 2}m,
\\z& = 1 -\phantom{ 2}m;\ m\in \mathbb{R}
\\ \end{aligned}\)}{\(\begin{aligned}[t] x& =\phantom{ -}4 + 2k, &
\\y& =\phantom{ -}2 +\phantom{ 2}k,
\\z& = -1 -\phantom{ 2}k;\ k\in \mathbb{R}
\\ \end{aligned}\)}{\(\begin{aligned}[t] x& = -2 + 2u, &
\\y& =\phantom{ -}2,
\\z& =\phantom{ -}1 - 2u;\ u\in \mathbb{R}
\\ \end{aligned}\)}{}{}}
\LANGpl{
\Question{
Dane sńÖ punkty \(A = [0;0;1]\),
\(B = [2;0;-1]\) i
\(S = [2;1;0]\),
wyznacz r√≥wnanie parametryczne obrazu prostej 
\(AB\) w symetrii wzglńôdem 
punktu \(S\).}
{\(\begin{aligned}[t] x& =\phantom{ -}4 + t, &
\\y& =\phantom{ -}2,
\\z& = -1 - t;\ t\in \mathbb{R}
\\ \end{aligned}\)}{\(\begin{aligned}[t] x& = 2 + 2m, &
\\y& = 2 +\phantom{ 2}m,
\\z& = 1 -\phantom{ 2}m;\ m\in \mathbb{R}
\\ \end{aligned}\)}{\(\begin{aligned}[t] x& =\phantom{ -}4 + 2k, &
\\y& =\phantom{ -}2 +\phantom{ 2}k,
\\z& = -1 -\phantom{ 2}k;\ k\in \mathbb{R}
\\ \end{aligned}\)}{\(\begin{aligned}[t] x& = -2 + 2u, &
\\y& =\phantom{ -}2,
\\z& =\phantom{ -}1 - 2u;\ u\in \mathbb{R}
\\ \end{aligned}\)}{}{}}
\LANGcs{
\Question{
Jsou d√°ny body \(A = [0;0;1]\) ;
\(B = [2;0;-1]\) a
\(S = [2;1;0]\).
Urńćete parametrick√© vyj√°dŇôen√≠ pŇô√≠mky, kter√° je obrazem pŇô√≠mky \(AB\) ve stŇôedov√© soumńõrnosti se stŇôedem v bodńõ \(S\).}

\\y& =\phantom{ -}2,
\\z& = -1 - t;\ t\in \mathbb{R}
\\ \end{aligned}\)}{\(\begin{aligned}[t] x& = 2 + 2m, &
\\y& = 2 +\phantom{ 2}m,
\\z& = 1 -\phantom{ 2}m;\ m\in \mathbb{R}
\\ \end{aligned}\)}{\(\begin{aligned}[t] x& =\phantom{ -}4 + 2k, &
\\y& =\phantom{ -}2 +\phantom{ 2}k,
\\z& = -1 -\phantom{ 2}k;\  k\in \mathbb{R}
\\ \end{aligned}\)}{\(\begin{aligned}[t] x& = -2 + 2u, &
\\y& =\phantom{ -}2,
